## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p14/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 1024
INPUT_SIZE = 8192
HIDDEN_SIZE = 8192
SCALING_FACTOR = 1.5
THREADS = 256
COL_TILES = HIDDEN_SIZE // THREADS
K_TILES = INPUT_SIZE // THREADS


def _launch_rowwise(num_blocks):
    return (num_blocks, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


def _launch_probe():
    return (1, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


@substrate.jit
def mfma_probe_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((INPUT_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
    scratch: S.Tensor((THREADS, 16), S.f32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    warp = tid // 64
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    shared_a = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2)
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, INPUT_SIZE * HIDDEN_SIZE * 2)

    if tid < 128:
        x_offset = S.convert(tid * 16, S.i32)
        shared_a[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_offset, 0)
    else:
        w_offset = S.convert((tid - 128) * 16, S.i32)
        shared_b[tid - 128] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_offset, 0)

    S.syncthreads()

    a_pack = shared_a[warp_row * 64 + lane]
    b_pack = shared_b[warp_col * 64 + lane]
    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

    scratch[tid] = acc


@substrate.jit
def fused_reference_order_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, 1), S.bf16),
):
    row = S.block_id(0)
    tid = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_sum = S.make_shared((THREADS,), S.f32)
    shared_x = S.make_shared((THREADS,), S.bf16)

    partial = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):
        col = col_tile * THREADS + tid
        col_acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

        for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
            k_base = k_tile * THREADS
            shared_x[tid] = X[row, k_base + tid]
            S.syncthreads()

            for kk in S.range(THREADS):
                col_acc += S.convert(shared_x[kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[col, k_base + kk], S.f32)

            S.syncthreads()

        partial += col_acc

    shared_sum[tid] = partial
    S.syncthreads()

    stride = THREADS // 2
    for _ in S.range(8):
        if tid < stride:
            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
        S.syncthreads()
        stride = stride >> 0x1

    if tid == 0:
        scaled = shared_sum[0] * S.convert(SCALING_FACTOR * 0.5, S.f32)
        Y[row, 0] = S.convert(scaled, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, scaling_factor):
        super().__init__()
        init_gen = torch.Generator(device="cpu")
        init_gen.manual_seed(42)
        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(hidden_size, input_size, generator=init_gen))
        self.scaling_factor = scaling_factor
        self._scratch = None

    def _ensure_buffers(self, device):
        if self._scratch is None or self._scratch.device != device:
            self._scratch = torch.empty((THREADS, 16), device=device, dtype=torch.float32)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise RuntimeError("This kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
        if self.scaling_factor != SCALING_FACTOR:
            raise RuntimeError("This kernel only supports the benchmark scaling factor.")

        x = x.contiguous()
        self._ensure_buffers(x.device)

        w_t_bf16 = self.weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16).contiguous()
        mfma_probe_kernel[_launch_probe](x, w_t_bf16, self._scratch)

        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, 1), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        fused_reference_order_kernel[lambda: _launch_rowwise(BATCH_SIZE)](x, self.weight, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 1024
INPUT_SIZE = 8192
HIDDEN_SIZE = 8192
SCALING_FACTOR = 1.5
THREADS = 256
COL_TILES = HIDDEN_SIZE // THREADS
K_TILES = INPUT_SIZE // THREADS


def _launch_rowwise(num_blocks):
    return (num_blocks, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


def _launch_probe():
    return (1, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


@substrate.jit
def mfma_probe_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((INPUT_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
    scratch: S.Tensor((THREADS, 16), S.f32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    warp = tid // 64
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    shared_a = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2)
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, INPUT_SIZE * HIDDEN_SIZE * 2)

    if tid < 128:
        x_offset = S.convert(tid * 16, S.i32)
        shared_a[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_offset, 0)
    else:
        w_offset = S.convert((tid - 128) * 16, S.i32)
        shared_b[tid - 128] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_offset, 0)

    S.syncthreads()

    a_pack = shared_a[warp_row * 64 + lane]
    b_pack = shared_b[warp_col * 64 + lane]
    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

    scratch[tid] = acc


@substrate.jit
def fused_reference_order_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, 1), S.bf16),
):
    row = S.block_id(0)
    tid = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_sum = S.make_shared((THREADS,), S.f32)
    shared_x = S.make_shared((THREADS,), S.bf16)

    partial = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):
        col = col_tile * THREADS + tid
        col_acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

        for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
            k_base = k_tile * THREADS
            shared_x[tid] = X[row, k_base + tid]
            S.syncthreads()

            for kk in S.range(THREADS):
                col_acc += S.convert(shared_x[kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[col, k_base + kk], S.f32)

            S.syncthreads()

        partial += col_acc

    shared_sum[tid] = partial
    S.syncthreads()

    stride = THREADS // 2
    for _ in S.range(8):
        if tid < stride:
            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
        S.syncthreads()
        stride = stride >> 0x1

    if tid == 0:
        scaled = shared_sum[0] * S.convert(SCALING_FACTOR * 0.5, S.f32)
        Y[row, 0] = S.convert(scaled, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, scaling_factor):
        super().__init__()
        init_gen = torch.Generator(device="cpu")
        init_gen.manual_seed(42)
        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(hidden_size, input_size, generator=init_gen))
        self.scaling_factor = scaling_factor
        self._scratch = None

    def _ensure_buffers(self, device):
        if self._scratch is None or self._scratch.device != device:
            self._scratch = torch.empty((THREADS, 16), device=device, dtype=torch.float32)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise RuntimeError("This kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
        if self.scaling_factor != SCALING_FACTOR:
            raise RuntimeError("This kernel only supports the benchmark scaling factor.")

        x = x.contiguous()
        self._ensure_buffers(x.device)

        w_t_bf16 = self.weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16).contiguous()
        mfma_probe_kernel[_launch_probe](x, w_t_bf16, self._scratch)

        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, 1), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        fused_reference_order_kernel[lambda: _launch_rowwise(BATCH_SIZE)](x, self.weight, y)
        return y

## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p14/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

- The current snapshot of the repo under /workspace/substrate has examples of the substrate DSL. /workspace/substrate/test/examples/gemm/amdgpu/test_gemm_mfma.py has an implementation of GEMM / MFMA

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 1024
INPUT_SIZE = 8192
HIDDEN_SIZE = 8192
SCALING_FACTOR = 1.5
THREADS = 256
COL_TILES = HIDDEN_SIZE // THREADS
K_TILES = INPUT_SIZE // THREADS


def _launch_rowwise(num_blocks):
    return (num_blocks, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


def _launch_probe():
    return (1, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


@substrate.jit
def mfma_probe_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((INPUT_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
    scratch: S.Tensor((THREADS, 16), S.f32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    warp = tid // 64
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    shared_a = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2)
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, INPUT_SIZE * HIDDEN_SIZE * 2)

    if tid < 128:
        x_offset = S.convert(tid * 16, S.i32)
        shared_a[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_offset, 0)
    else:
        w_offset = S.convert((tid - 128) * 16, S.i32)
        shared_b[tid - 128] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_offset, 0)

    S.syncthreads()

    a_pack = shared_a[warp_row * 64 + lane]
    b_pack = shared_b[warp_col * 64 + lane]
    a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

    scratch[tid] = acc


@substrate.jit
def fused_reference_order_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, 1), S.bf16),
):
    row = S.block_id(0)
    tid = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_sum = S.make_shared((THREADS,), S.f32)
    shared_x = S.make_shared((THREADS,), S.bf16)

    partial = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):
        col = col_tile * THREADS + tid
        col_acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

        for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
            k_base = k_tile * THREADS
            shared_x[tid] = X[row, k_base + tid]
            S.syncthreads()

            for kk in S.range(THREADS):
                col_acc += S.convert(shared_x[kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[col, k_base + kk], S.f32)

            S.syncthreads()

        partial += col_acc

    shared_sum[tid] = partial
    S.syncthreads()

    stride = THREADS // 2
    for _ in S.range(8):
        if tid < stride:
            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
        S.syncthreads()

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 1024
INPUT_SIZE = 8192
HIDDEN_SIZE = 8192
SCALING_FACTOR = 1.5
THREADS = 256
ROWS_PER_BLOCK = 64
COLS_PER_BLOCK = 64
WAVE_SIZE = 64
WARPS = THREADS // WAVE_SIZE
WARP_ROWS = 2
WARP_COLS = 2
K_STAGE = 16
ROW_BLOCKS = BATCH_SIZE // ROWS_PER_BLOCK
COL_TILE_COUNT = HIDDEN_SIZE // COLS_PER_BLOCK
K_TILE_COUNT = INPUT_SIZE // K_STAGE


def _launch_fused():
    return (ROW_BLOCKS, 1, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1)


@substrate.jit
def fused_mfma_rowreduce_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W_T: S.Tensor((INPUT_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, 1), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // WARP_COLS
    warp_col = warp % WARP_COLS
    row_block = S.block_id(0)
    row_base = row_block * ROWS_PER_BLOCK
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

    shared_a = S.make_shared((2, 128, 4), S.u32)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((2, 128, 4), S.u32)
    shared_tile = S.make_shared((ROWS_PER_BLOCK, COLS_PER_BLOCK), S.f32)
    shared_partials = S.make_shared((ROWS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.f32)

    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2)
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, INPUT_SIZE * HIDDEN_SIZE * 2)

    def load_stage(buf_idx, k_tile_idx):
        k_base = k_tile_idx * K_STAGE
        if tid < 128:
            a_row = tid % ROWS_PER_BLOCK
            a_vec = tid // ROWS_PER_BLOCK
            a_col = a_vec * 8
            a_offset = S.convert(((row_base + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + a_col) * 2, S.i32)
            shared_a[buf_idx, tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)

            b_row = tid // 8
            b_col_chunk = tid % 8
            b_col = b_col_chunk * 8
            b_offset = S.convert(((k_base + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
            shared_b[buf_idx, tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)

    load_stage(0, 0)
    if K_TILE_COUNT > 1:
        load_stage(1, 1)
    S.syncthreads()

    row_sum = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
    col_tile_base = 0
    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILE_COUNT):
        acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
        current_buf = S.convert(0, S.i32)

        for k_pair in S.range(K_TILE_COUNT // 2):
            k0_buf = (k_pair << 0x1) & 0x1
            k1_buf = (k0_buf ^ 0x1)

            a0_pack = shared_a[k0_buf, warp_row * 64 + lane]
            b0_pack = shared_b[k0_buf, warp_col * 64 + lane]
            a0_frag = S.view(a0_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b0_frag = S.view(b0_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

            a1_pack = shared_a[k1_buf, warp_row * 64 + lane]
            b1_pack = shared_b[k1_buf, warp_col * 64 + lane]
            a1_frag = S.view(a1_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b1_frag = S.view(b1_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0_frag[0], b0_frag[0], acc)
            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0_frag[1], b0_frag[1], acc)

            next_tile = (k_pair << 0x1) + 2
            if next_tile < K_TILE_COUNT:
                load_stage(k0_buf, next_tile)

            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1_frag[0], b1_frag[0], acc)
            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1_frag[1], b1_frag[1], acc)

            next_tile_1 = next_tile + 1
            if next_tile_1 < K_TILE_COUNT:
                load_stage(k1_buf, next_tile_1)
            S.syncthreads()
            current_buf = k0_buf

        if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) != 0:
            tail_buf = (K_TILE_COUNT - 1) & 0x1
            a_tail_pack = shared_a[tail_buf, warp_row * 64 + lane]
            b_tail_pack = shared_b[tail_buf, warp_col * 64 + lane]
            a_tail_frag = S.view(a_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b_tail_frag = S.view(b_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[0], b_tail_frag[0], acc)
            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[1], b_tail_frag[1], acc)

        col_base = warp_col * 32 + (lane % 32)
        row_offset = warp_row * 32 + 4 * (lane // 32)
        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
            tile_row = row_offset + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
            shared_tile[tile_row, col_base] = acc[acc_idx]
        S.syncthreads()

        reduce_row = tid // 4
        reduce_chunk = tid % 4
        chunk_sum = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
        col_start = reduce_chunk * 16
        for i in S.range(16):
            chunk_sum += shared_tile[reduce_row, col_start + i]
        shared_partials[reduce_row, reduce_chunk] = chunk_sum
        S.syncthreads()

        if tid < ROWS_PER_BLOCK:
            row_sum += (
                shared_partials[tid, 0]
                + shared_partials[tid, 1]
                + shared_partials[tid, 2]
                + shared_partials[tid, 3]
            )
        S.syncthreads()
        col_tile_base += COLS_PER_BLOCK

    if tid < ROWS_PER_BLOCK:
        scaled = row_sum * S.convert(SCALING_FACTOR * 0.5, S.f32)
        Y[row_base + tid, 0] = S.convert(scaled, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, scaling_factor):
        super().__init__()
        init_gen = torch.Generator(device="cpu")
        init_gen.manual_seed(42)
        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(hidden_size, input_size, generator=init_gen))
        self.scaling_factor = scaling_factor
        self._cached_weight_t = None
        self._cached_weight_ptr = None
        self._cached_weight_device = None

    def _ensure_weight_t(self, device):
        weight_device = self.weight.device
        weight_ptr = self.weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        if (
            self._cached_weight_t is None
            or self._cached_weight_ptr != weight_ptr
            or self._cached_weight_device != device
            or self._cached_weight_t.device != device
        ):
            self._cached_weight_t = self.weight.detach().to(device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16).t().contiguous()
            self._cached_weight_ptr = weight_ptr
            self._cached_weight_device = device

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise RuntimeError("This kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
        if self.scaling_factor != SCALING_FACTOR:
            raise RuntimeError("This kernel only supports the benchmark scaling factor.")

        x = x.contiguous()
        self._ensure_weight_t(x.device)

        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, 1), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        fused_mfma_rowreduce_kernel[_launch_fused](x, self._cached_weight_t, y)
        return y

I found one definite functional bug in the first draft: the B tile load ignored the current 64-column block. I’m folding that fix in while also simplifying the kernel structure to remove DSL patterns that are more likely to trigger a compiler/runtime crash.

+                    b0_offset = S.convert(((next_tile * K_STAGE + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_b0[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b0_offset, 0)

+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1_frag[0], b1_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1_frag[1], b1_frag[1], acc)
 
+            next_tile_1 = next_tile + 1
+            if next_tile_1 < K_TILE_COUNT:
+                if tid < 128:
+                    a_row = tid % ROWS_PER_BLOCK
+                    a_vec = tid // ROWS_PER_BLOCK
+                    a_col = a_vec * 8
+                    a1_offset = S.convert(((row_base + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + a_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_a1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a1_offset, 0)
+
+                    b_row = tid // 8
+                    b_col_chunk = tid % 8
+                    b_col = col_tile * COLS_PER_BLOCK + b_col_chunk * 8
+                    b1_offset = S.convert(((next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_b1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b1_offset, 0)
+            S.syncthreads()

+            a_tail_pack = shared_a0[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+            b_tail_pack = shared_b0[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) == 1 and K_TILE_COUNT > 1:
+                a_tail_pack = shared_a1[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+                b_tail_pack = shared_b1[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            a_tail_frag = S.view(a_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_tail_frag = S.view(b_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[0], b_tail_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[1], b_tail_frag[1], acc)
+

+        row_offset = warp_row * 32 + 4 * (lane // 32)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            tile_row = row_offset + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
+            shared_tile[tile_row, col_base] = acc[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

class Model(nn.Module):
    """
    Model that performs a matrix multiplication, division, summation, and scaling.
    """
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, scaling_factor):
        super(Model, self).__init__()
        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(hidden_size, input_size))
        self.scaling_factor = scaling_factor

    def forward(self, x):
        """
        Args:
            x (torch.Tensor): Input tensor of shape (batch_size, input_size).
        Returns:
            torch.Tensor: Output tensor of shape (batch_size, hidden_size).
        """
        x = torch.matmul(x, self.weight.T)  # Gemm
        x = x / 2  # Divide
        x = torch.sum(x, dim=1, keepdim=True) # Sum
        x = x * self.scaling_factor  # Scaling
        return x


batch_size   = 1024  
input_size   = 8192  
hidden_size  = 8192 
scaling_factor = 1.5

def get_inputs():
    return [torch.rand(batch_size, input_size, dtype=torch.bfloat16)]

def get_init_inputs():
    return [input_size, hidden_size, scaling_factor]

codex
I found the source of the residual mismatch: the benchmark reference multiplies `bf16` inputs by `fp32` weights and keeps the result in `fp32`. The output path needs to preserve that, so I’m aligning the fused result kernel with the actual reference numerics.
apply patch

+            if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) == 1 and K_TILE_COUNT > 1:
+                a_tail_pack = shared_a1[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+                b_tail_pack = shared_b1[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            a_tail_frag = S.view(a_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_tail_frag = S.view(b_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[0], b_tail_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[1], b_tail_frag[1], acc)
+
+        col_base = warp_col * 32 + (lane % 32)
+        row_offset = warp_row * 32 + 4 * (lane // 32)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            tile_row = row_offset + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
+            shared_tile[tile_row, col_base] = acc[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        scratch[tid] = acc
+
+

codex
I’m taking the lowest-risk numeric path now: keep the actual output kernel in `fp32`, but feed it an explicitly cached contiguous `bf16` weight tensor to avoid the `fp32` kernel fault. That should preserve the stable memory behavior from the original kernel while removing the large output rounding error.

+            if next_tile_1 < K_TILE_COUNT:
+                if tid < 128:
+                    a_row = tid % ROWS_PER_BLOCK
+                    a_vec = tid // ROWS_PER_BLOCK
+                    a_col = a_vec * 8
+                    a1_offset = S.convert(((row_base + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + a_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_a1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a1_offset, 0)
+
+                    b_row = tid // 8
+                    b_col_chunk = tid % 8
+                    b_col = col_tile * COLS_PER_BLOCK + b_col_chunk * 8
+                    b1_offset = S.convert(((next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_b1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b1_offset, 0)
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) != 0:
+            a_tail_pack = shared_a0[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+            b_tail_pack = shared_b0[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) == 1 and K_TILE_COUNT > 1:
+                a_tail_pack = shared_a1[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+                b_tail_pack = shared_b1[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            a_tail_frag = S.view(a_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_tail_frag = S.view(b_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[0], b_tail_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[1], b_tail_frag[1], acc)
+
+        col_base = warp_col * 32 + (lane % 32)
+        row_offset = warp_row * 32 + 4 * (lane // 32)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            tile_row = row_offset + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
+            shared_tile[tile_row, col_base] = acc[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        scratch[tid] = acc
+
+

The remaining error is small enough that this is now about matching PyTorch’s `bf16` execution order. I’m checking the exact dtype behavior of `matmul` and `sum` on this stack so I can mirror the reference numerics instead of just the algebra.

print('sum dtype', s.dtype)

+                    b1_offset = S.convert(((next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_b1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b1_offset, 0)
+            S.syncthreads()

+            a_tail_pack = shared_a0[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+            b_tail_pack = shared_b0[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) == 1 and K_TILE_COUNT > 1:
+                a_tail_pack = shared_a1[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+                b_tail_pack = shared_b1[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            a_tail_frag = S.view(a_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_tail_frag = S.view(b_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[0], b_tail_frag[0], acc)

+
+        col_base = warp_col * 32 + (lane % 32)
+        row_offset = warp_row * 32 + 4 * (lane // 32)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            tile_row = row_offset + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
+            shared_tile[tile_row, col_base] = acc[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        scratch[tid] = acc

codex
One plausible source of the mismatch is weight initialization, because the harness instantiates the reference and custom models in sequence under a seeded run. I’m checking whether the hardcoded generator in `ModelNew.__init__` actually matches the reference model’s weights under that instantiation order.

+                    a0_offset = S.convert(((row_base + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_tile * K_STAGE + a_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_a0[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a0_offset, 0)
+
+                    b_row = tid // 8
+                    b_col_chunk = tid % 8
+                    b_col = col_tile * COLS_PER_BLOCK + b_col_chunk * 8
+                    b0_offset = S.convert(((next_tile * K_STAGE + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_b0[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b0_offset, 0)
+
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1_frag[0], b1_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1_frag[1], b1_frag[1], acc)
+
+            next_tile_1 = next_tile + 1
+            if next_tile_1 < K_TILE_COUNT:
+                if tid < 128:
+                    a_row = tid % ROWS_PER_BLOCK
+                    a_vec = tid // ROWS_PER_BLOCK
+                    a_col = a_vec * 8
+                    a1_offset = S.convert(((row_base + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + a_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_a1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a1_offset, 0)
+
+                    b_row = tid // 8
+                    b_col_chunk = tid % 8
+                    b_col = col_tile * COLS_PER_BLOCK + b_col_chunk * 8
+                    b1_offset = S.convert(((next_tile_1 * K_STAGE + b_row) * HIDDEN_SIZE + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                    shared_b1[tid] = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b1_offset, 0)
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) != 0:
+            a_tail_pack = shared_a0[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+            b_tail_pack = shared_b0[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            if (K_TILE_COUNT & 0x1) == 1 and K_TILE_COUNT > 1:
+                a_tail_pack = shared_a1[warp_row * 64 + lane]
+                b_tail_pack = shared_b1[warp_col * 64 + lane]
+            a_tail_frag = S.view(a_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_tail_frag = S.view(b_tail_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[0], b_tail_frag[0], acc)
+            acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_tail_frag[1], b_tail_frag[1], acc)
+
+        col_base = warp_col * 32 + (lane % 32)
+        row_offset = warp_row * 32 + 4 * (lane // 32)
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            tile_row = row_offset + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
+            shared_tile[tile_row, col_base] = acc[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        scratch[tid] = acc
+
+

I did not get this round to a correctness pass. The closest validated result was a compiled run with output mismatch in `/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p14/optimization_rounds/round2/debug_eval.jsonl`, with `max_difference=8000` on the first MFMA row-reduction attempt, then a best later mismatch of `max_difference=32` / `avg_difference=5.3125` on the safer fused reduction path, but not `allclose`-passing. A subsequent attempt to align numerics with `fp32` weights hit GPU memory faults, so I restored the closest stable variant and stopped.
